Policy reminder: Handling confidential employee information Please remember that any discussion regarding an employee’s medical, psychological, or family circumstances must remain strictly confidential. Even if the information was shared informally or “in confidence,” redistributing it in any form violates our data protection standards. Gossip of this nature erodes trust and invites liability. If you’re uncertain whether something can be discussed, err on the side of silence and consult HR.
